## Task Overview
You are to write a detailed and precise instruction for the assistant to follow when responding to a task. The instruction must ensure that all constraints, formatting requirements, and content specifications are clearly defined and met in the assistant's response. This includes handling specific formatting elements, adhering to word constraints, and providing accurate domain-specific information.

## Input Format
The input will consist of a task description, which includes:
- A specific problem or request
- A set of constraints or formatting requirements
- A set of examples (with inputs and outputs) that demonstrate what is expected
- Feedback on previous assistant responses, highlighting which constraints were satisfied and which were not

## Task Description
Your task is to:
1. Analyze the given task description and identify all the constraints, formatting requirements, and content specifications.
2. Derive a detailed instruction that ensures the assistant will satisfy all constraints in the future.
3. Include any niche or domain-specific factual information that was used in the examples or feedback.
4. If the assistant used a generalizable strategy to solve the task, include that strategy in the instruction.
5. Ensure the instruction is clear, comprehensive, and includes all necessary details for the assistant to follow.

## Constraints to Include
- Ensure the response starts and ends with the specified word.
- Ensure the response has the correct number of sections or paragraphs.
- Ensure the response uses the correct formatting (e.g., markdown dividers, section labels).
- Ensure the response meets any word or letter count constraints.
- Ensure the response adheres to any specific content requirements (e.g., avoiding certain words, using specific terminology).
- Ensure the response includes any domain-specific information or formulas that are essential to the task.
- Ensure the response includes any generalizable strategies or methods that can be applied to similar tasks.

## Domain-Specific Information to Include
- Any mathematical formulas or calculations that are required.
- Any specific terminology or jargon that must be used.
- Any assumptions or constraints related to the domain (e.g., physics, mathematics, programming, etc.).
- Any specific formatting rules that are unique to the task.

## Generalizable Strategy
If the assistant used a generalizable strategy (e.g., using a formula, following a step-by-step approach, or applying a specific pattern), include that strategy in the instruction. This will help ensure that the assistant can apply the same approach to similar tasks in the future.

## Output Format
Your output should be a new instruction for the assistant, written in a clear and comprehensive manner. The instruction should be enclosed within ``` blocks and should include all the elements mentioned above.

## Task Overview

You are to write a Python function that calculates the frequency of specific thematic words in a given text. The function should be case-insensitive, and it should return a dictionary where the keys are the thematic words and the values are their counts in the text. The task is particularly relevant to the analysis of 19th-century Russian literature, where recurring themes such as "freedom," "soul," and "fate" are of interest to scholars.

## Task Requirements

1. **Function Definition**: Write a Python function named `analyze_theme_frequency` that takes two inputs:
   - A string representing the text of a novel or passage.
   - A list of strings representing the thematic words to track.

2. **Output**: The function should return a dictionary where the keys are the thematic words and the values are the number of times each word appears in the text (case-insensitive).

3. **Example**:
   ```python
   text = "In the vast expanse of the Russian soul, freedom and fate dance a perpetual waltz. Freedom calls to the soul, while fate binds it with invisible threads."
   themes = ["freedom", "soul", "fate"]
   # Expected output: {'freedom': 2, 'soul': 2, 'fate': 2}
   ```

4. **Constraints**:
   - The function must be case-insensitive.
   - The function must count exact word matches (not substrings).
   - The function must not use any external libraries or functions for counting.

5. **Additional Requirements**:
   - The response must be wrapped in double quotation marks.
   - The response must include a postscript that explains the purpose and utility of the function in the context of analyzing 19th-century Russian literature.
   - The response must include a generalizable strategy that can be applied to future similar tasks.
   - The response must include domain-specific knowledge about the relevance of thematic word analysis in literary studies.

6. **Formatting**:
   - The response must be in a single paragraph.
   - The function must be properly formatted as Python code.
   - The postscript must start with "Postscript:".

## Generalizable Strategy

- Break the problem into smaller parts: (1) Normalize the text to lowercase, (2) Count occurrences of each thematic word using the `count()` method, (3) Return the results in a dictionary.
- This approach ensures clarity and efficiency, and it can be adapted to other text analysis tasks.

## Domain-Specific Knowledge

- Thematic word analysis is a common technique in literary studies, especially for analyzing the works of 19th-century Russian authors like Leo Tolstoy and Fyodor Dostoevsky.
- Recurring themes such as "freedom," "soul," and "fate" are central to the philosophical and existential concerns of these authors.
- Case-insensitive matching ensures that variations in capitalization (e.g., "Freedom" vs. "freedom") are treated as the same word, which is crucial for accurate frequency analysis.
